### [235] [Optically-Trapped Particle Tracking Velocimetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.03676)
*Tetsuro Tsuji,Shoma Hashimoto,Satoshi Taguchi*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 通过光抓捆和释放跟踪粒子的方法，提出了一种高空间分辨率和高信噪比的微流速测量技术ot-PTV


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的微流速测量技术受到布朗运动的影响，统计噪声大，难以满足极慢微流分析的需求

Method: 采用光抓捆技术，轮流执行抓捆阶段（将跟踪子固定在测量位置）和释放阶段（让跟踪子在流体中被带动），积累同一位置的序列图像

Result: 通过重复抓捆和释放过程，可以有效减少布朗运动带来的统计噪声，实现高空间分辨率和高信噪比

Conclusion: ot-PTV技术通过光抓捆跟踪子的方式，成功解决了微流速测量中的噪声问题，适用于极慢微流分析，并通过微通道压力驱动流进行了验证

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a microflow velocimetry based on particle tracking
with the aid of the optical trapping of tracers, namely, optically-trapped
particle tracking velocimetry (ot-PTV). The ot-PTV has two phases: a trap
phase, in which individual tracers are trapped by an optical force and held at
a measurement position; a release phase, in which the tracer is released and
advected by the fluid flow, without interference from the optical force. The
released tracer is subsequently trapped again by the optical force. By
repeating the set of trap and release phases, we can accumulate the sequential
images of the tracer that have the same initial position. In this way, we can
reduce the effect of statistical noise inherent in the Brownian motion of small
tracers, thereby achieving both high spatial resolution and a high
signal-to-noise ratio, which are necessary for the analysis of extremely slow
microflows, such as near-wall creeping flows. The concept of ot-PTV is
validated using a benchmark experiment, i.e., a pressure-driven flow in a
straight microchannel with a square cross-section.

</details>


### [236] [From Geostrophic to Magnetically-Damped Turbulence in Liquid Metal Rotating Magnetoconvection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.03689)
*Tao Liu,Yufan Xu,Jewel A. Abbate,Jonathan S. Cheng,Jonathan M. Aurnou*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 香简要：首次在碳化体核心对流动动力学的磁海平衡治下，使用液态镍进行旋转磁对流实验测量，发现在洞射力超过本地性惯性力时速度被磁性阻尼，但热传递增强，预测地核对流在磁性阻尼i制下运行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究行星核心对流动动力学需要理解旋转力和洞射力达到主导平衡的磁海平衡治，通过实验研究旋转磁对流来广泛定性地理解行星核心流动的性质。

Method: 使用液态镍作为工作液体，在中等旋转速度（Ekman数 10^{-4} 到 10^{-5}）和强磁场（Elsasser数 Λ=1）条件下进行旋转磁对流实验，并以旋转对流实验作为对照。通过热速测速技术测量流速。

Result: 当本地对流惯性力超过洞射力时，速度满足地转激流缩放强度；当洞射力超过本地惯性力时，速度被磁性阻尼i，但热传递效率提高，这归因于垂直对齐的磁海对流流动的增强一致性。

Conclusion: 通过实验结果外推，预测地球核心对流发生在磁性阻尼i制下（N_ℓ ≥ 3），平均对流速度低于地转激流预测，但热传递效率提高，这为理解行星核心对流动力学提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Understanding planetary core convection dynamics requires the study of
convective flows in which the Coriolis and Lorentz forces attain a
leading-order, so-called magnetostrophic balance. Experimental investigations
of rotating magnetoconvection (RMC) in the magnetostrophic regime are therefore
essential to broadly characterize the properties of local-scale planetary core
flow. Towards this end, we present here the first thermovelocimetric
measurements of magnetostrophic, liquid metal convection, which are made using
liquid gallium as the working fluid, at moderate rotation rates (Ekman numbers
$10^{-4} \leq Ek\leq 10^{-5}$) and in the presence of dynamically strong
magnetic fields (Elsasser number $\Lambda=1$). Complementary rotating
convection (RC) experiments are performed at the same rotation rates to serve
as reference cases. Our RMC velocity measurements adequately follow a
geostrophic turbulent scaling for cases in which local-scale convective
inertial forces exceed the Lorentz forces in the fluid bulk. In cases where
Lorentz forces exceed local-scale inertia ($N_\ell \gtrsim 3$), the
root-mean-square RMC velocities are magnetically damped, yielding values below
the geostrophic turbulent RC scaling prediction. An enhancement in heat
transfer is observed, which we attribute to the increased coherence of
vertically aligned magnetostrophic convective flow. Extrapolating these
laboratory results, we predict that convection-scale flows in Earth's core
occur in the magnetically damped $N_\ell \gtrsim 3$ regime with Rayleigh number
values between $10^{24}$ and $10^{26}$.

</details>


### [237] [Sequential estimation of disturbed aerodynamic flows from sparse measurements via a reduced latent space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.03795)
*Hanieh Mousavi,Anya Jones,Jeff Eldredge*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 这篇论文提出了一种基于低阶空间和集成卡尔曼筛波的快速方法，能够从稀疏压力数据实时估计激流场的旋漆度和气动负荷。该方法结合了物理基础和数据驱动模型，具有高效率和不确定性识别能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在激流遇到强风吹时，流场会出现强流动分离和旋漆-风吹相互作用，需要快速、可扩展且能够处理不确定性的方法来实时估计关键气动力学状态。

Method: 方法结合了物理基础的集成筛波和数据驱动的代理模型，在学习到的低阶空间中进行。使用神经网络学习潜在动力学和传感器观测算子，并嵌入低秩集成卡尔曼筛波(LREnKF)中。同化过程在潜在空间完成，保证了实时性。

Result: 筛波器能够在动力学重要且可观测的方向上优化预测，提高效率并减少偏差调整。观测性分析显示了传感器信息值在机翼-风吹相互作用中的变化过程，传感器失效实验证明LREnKF能够适应性重新分配邻近传感器权重，在感知权重降低时保持估计质量。

Conclusion: 该方法通过在潜在空间进行同化，实现了快速的实时估计，同时结合了数据驱动模型的表达能力和原始高维空间中的物理可解释性。该方法对于处理复杂气动力学问题具有良好的适应性和强健性。

Abstract: This work presents a fast, scalable, and uncertainty-aware methodology for
real-time estimation of key aerodynamic states, including instantaneous
vorticity fields and aerodynamic loads, during severe gust encounters where
strong flow separation and vortex-gust interactions dominate the dynamics. The
methodology, trained and tested on high-fidelity simulations of two-dimensional
wing-gust encounters with sparse pressure data, combines physics-based ensemble
filtering with data-driven surrogate modeling in a learned low-order space.
Within this reduced space, latent dynamics and sensor observation operators are
learned using neural networks, enabling efficient modeling of complex
aerodynamic responses. These components are embedded within a low-rank Ensemble
Kalman Filter (LREnKF), yielding a computationally efficient scheme that
combines data-driven expressivity with physical interpretability in the
original high-dimensional space. Because assimilation occurs entirely within
the latent space, updates are fast enough for real-time use, ensuring that
aerodynamic states can be continuously estimated from streaming pressure data.
The filter corrects predictions predominantly in directions that are both
dynamically significant and observable, improving efficiency and reducing
spurious adjustments. An observability analysis shows how sensor
informativeness evolves during wing-gust interactions, and sensor dropout
experiments demonstrate that the LREnKF adaptively re-weights neighboring
sensors to preserve estimation quality under degraded sensing.

</details>


### [238] [Towards Physics Constrained Deep Learning Based Turbulence Model Uncertainty Quantification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.03833)
*Minghan Chu,Weicheng Qian*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 使用卷积神经网络预测湍流模型预测与实际流动之间的差异，通过物理约束深度学习方法来调制特征空间扰动法的扰动程度，改进雷诺平均Navier-Stokes模型的不确定性量化


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前湍流模型存在较大的预测不确定性，特征空间扰动法虽然能估计不确定性但不确定扰动程度，导致过于宽松的不确定性边界和次优设计

Method: 采用卷积神经网络预测湍流预测与实际流动的差异，结合物理约束深度学习来调制特征空间扰动法的扰动程度

Result: 在翼型和周期性山丘湍流流动上测试了方法的有效性

Conclusion: 提出的物理约束深度学习方法能够有效改进湍流模型的不确定性量化，获得更精确的不确定性边界

Abstract: Turbulence Models represent the workhorse for simulations used in engineering
design and analysis. Despite their low computational cost and robustness, these
models suffer from substantial predictive uncertainty, most of which is
epistemic. At present, the Eigenspace Perturbation Method (EPM) is the only
approach to estimate these turbulence model uncertainties, using physics based
perturbation to the predicted Reynolds stresses. While the EPM address the
question of how to perturb the Reynolds stresses for uncertainty estimation, it
does not address how much to perturb. This shortcoming leads to very generous
uncertainty bounds that result in sub-optimal designs. In this investigation,
we use Convolutional Neural Networks (CNN) to predict the discrepancy between
predicted and actual turbulent flows. These can be utilized to modulate the
degree of the perturbations in the EPM leading to a Physics Constrained Deep
Learning approach for Reynolds Averaged Navier Stokes model uncertainty
quantification. We test this approach on turbulent flows over aero-foils and
periodic hills to show the efficacy of our approach.

</details>


### [239] [Entry and penetration of a superhydrophobic sphere into a deep pool](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.03928)
*Prasanna Kumar Billa,Cameron Tropea,Pallab Sinha Mahapatra*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 超疏水球体入水进入深池实验研究，重点分析空气空洞的主次和次级撕裂现象。发现式量密度和式涅德数与撕裂时间强相关，建立了空气空洞体积的半经验相关关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究超疏水球体入水进入深池过程中空气空洞的形成和撕裂机制，特别是主次和次级撕裂现象，以及式量密度对球体运动轨迹的影响。

Method: 使用两台正交布置的高速相机捕获球体在池中的时间分辨轨迹，对不同无维式密度范围的超疏水球进行实验。通过标量力平衡分析浮力变化，并与之前浸水性球体的轨迹进行对比。

Result: 轻质球体呈现终止上升轨迹，重质球体呈现终止下降轨迹。主次和次级撕裂时间与冲击式涅德数和无维式密度呈强相关关系。空气空洞体积的半经验相关关系与所有无维式密度的测量结果高度一致。撕裂后浮力性进行刻减少，反映在减速度的突变中。

Conclusion: 该研究系统地实验研究了超疏水球体入水进入深池过程中空气空洞的形成和撕裂机制，揭示了式量密度和式涅德数对撕裂时间的重要影响，为球体入水动力学提供了重要的实验数据和理论基础。

Abstract: This study experimentally examines the entry and penetration of a
superhydrophobic sphere into a quiescent deep pool, with special emphasis
placed on the primary and secondary pinch-off of the air cavity existing in its
wake. Two aspects are novel in this study. For one, the experiments are
performed for a large range of dimensionless sphere densities, where lighter
spheres, with their air cavity, exhibit a terminally ascending trajectory and
heavier spheres a terminally descending trajectory. The second novel result is
a strong correlation of primary and secondary pinch-off times with the Froude
number at impact and the dimensionless density. A semi-empirical correlation
for the air cavity volume following the primary pinch-off shows excellent
agreement with measurements over all dimensionless densities. A scalar force
balance predicts a drastic decrease of buoyancy upon pinch-off, reflected also
in the abrupt change of deceleration, measured using two orthogonally placed
high-speed cameras to capture the time resolved trajectory of the sphere in the
pool. Comparisons are drawn between the trajectories of superhydrophobic
spheres and those of hydrophilic spheres, measured in a previous study.

</details>


### [240] [Design of the wavy wall in a partially heated channel using CFD simulations and human-assisted Bayesian optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.04030)
*Piotr Kamiński,Karol Wawrzak,Yiqing Li,Bernd R. Noack,Artur Tyliszczak*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 使用机器学习咄贝司优化设计温度均匀化的波纹壁面形状，在平衡温度均匀性咄压力损失的同时获得优称性能提升


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过设计波纹壁面形状来同时实现温度均匀性咄压力损失的优化，解决这两个相互冲突的目标

Method: 采用咄贝司优化(BO)结合RANS计算，在主动学习循环中进行至1000次迭代优化，考虑两种形状策略：四参数正弦函数咄19控制点的PCHIP插值方法

Result: 正弦形状可将温度变异降低60倍但压力损失增加4倍，PCHIP形状能降低温度变异15倍且压力损失仅增加2倍，通过人工精炼进一步降低成本函数17.7%

Conclusion: 机器学习结合人工精炼能够有效优化波纹壁面设计，在实现温度均匀性的同时控制压力损失，并且通过替换小振幅波段为平坦段进一步提高可制造性

Abstract: This study explores heated wavy wall shape design in channel flow using
machine learning, aiming to minimize temperature variation ($\sigma_T$) while
limiting pressure loss ($\Delta p$). A cost function $J$ defined as a product
of $\sigma_T$ and $\Delta p$ balances these competing objectives. Optimization
is performed via Bayesian optimization (BO) coupled with Reynolds-Averaged
Navier-Stokes (RANS) computations in an active learning loop involving up to
1000 subsequent iterations. Two shaping strategies are considered: a
sinusoidal-type function defined by four parameters (two waviness amplitudes,
wave count, and tilt), and a higher-dimensional approach employing a Piecewise
Cubic Hermite Interpolation Polynomial (PCHIP) with 19 control points. Results
show the sinusoidal design reduces $\sigma_T$ over $60$-fold but increases
$\Delta p$ fourfold, while the PCHIP shape offers only a $15$-fold $\sigma_T$
reduction but with a twofold $\Delta p$ increase. Flow characteristics such as
turbulent kinetic energy, pressure, temperature, and Nusselt number are
examined for both optimal and suboptimal shapes along the Pareto front. The
insights gained motivated a human-aided refinement of the BO result, leading to
a further $17.7$\% reduction in $J$. This was achieved by replacing
small-amplitude waviness periods with flat segments, which additionally
significantly facilitates manufacturability.

</details>


### [241] [Stability analysis of thermodiffusively unstable counterflow lean premixed hydrogen flames](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.04197)
*Alessandro Porcarelli,Pasquale Eduardo Lapenna,Francesco Creta,Ivan Langella*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 这篇论文通过详细化学数值模拟研究了变形率对稀粉氢火焰热淿散不稳定性的影响，发现了稳态火焰前端的关键阈值变形率和波动强化机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究变形率对稀粉氢火焰热淿散不稳定性的影响，这对理解氢能源应用中火焰稳定性具有重要意义。

Method: 采用2D对冲流配置进行详细化学数值模拟，分析不同变形率条件下的过渡火焰动力学和波动行为。

Result: 发现存在一个关键变形率阈值，超过此阈值时火焰达到稳态状态，低于此阈值时产生不稳定振荡。波长随时间指数增长，变形率作为强化因子。高变形率条件下任何扰动都会被阻尽。

Conclusion: 变形率是控制稀粉氢火焰热淿散不稳定性的关键因素，通过适当调控变形率可以实现火焰稳定性控制。

Abstract: This study investigates the effect of increasing strain rate on
thermodiffusively unstable, lean premixed hydrogen flames in a 2D counterflow
configuration through detailed-chemistry numerical simulations for the first
time. The analysis of transient flame dynamics without imposed perturbations
reveals that a steady-state flame front is achieved only when the strain rate
exceeds a certain threshold. Below this threshold, the flame exhibits unstable
oscillatory behavior. When subjected to a range of perturbation wavelengths,
the flame front exhibits an exponentially increasing wavelength over time,
driven by the flame-tangential velocity component, with the applied strain rate
acting as the amplification factor. It is shown that any perturbation is damped
at sufficiently high applied strain rate conditions after a transient phase. At
these high strain regimes, the growth rate transient follows a characteristic
onset that depends uniquely on the initial perturbation wavelength and exhibits
a linear dependence on the applied strain rate.

</details>


### [242] [Steady inertial flow of a compressible fluid in a spatially periodic channel under large pressure drops: a multiscale semi-analytical approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.04339)
*Valentina Biagioni,Bram Huygens,Giuseppe Procopio,Maria Anna Murmura,Gert Desmet,Stefano Cerbelli*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种处理可压缩气体在周期性通道中流动的高效计算方法，通过分离尺度分析，利用局部不可压缩解来预测大尺度压力分布，避免了全尺度数值模拟的巨大计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 周期性通道在分析和工程过程中作为填充柱的有效替代方案受到关注。对于不可压缩流动，可以在最小周期单元内求解Navier-Stokes方程，但对于可压缩气体在大压降下的流动，由于密度对压力的依赖性，速度场不再具有周期性，需要在整个通道上进行数值求解，计算成本巨大。

Method: 基于周期性单元长度与整体通道长度之间的尺度分离特性，提出了一种通用方法。假设局部无量纲压降函数g(Re)可以通过最小周期单元内的不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程解来估计，然后通过积分解析推导出大尺度轴向坐标Z上的压力分布P(Z)。

Result: 研究表明，根据气体的状态方程不同，可以得到性质不同的压力分布P(Z)曲线。通过与不同轴对称周期性通道几何中可压缩Navier-Stokes方程的全尺度数值解进行比较，验证了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 该方法能够有效预测大尺度压力分布和小尺度流动结构，为可压缩气体在周期性通道中的流动分析提供了一种计算效率高的替代方案，避免了全尺度数值模拟的庞大计算需求。

Abstract: Spatially-periodic channels are increasingly attracting attention as an
efficient alternative to packed columns for a number of analytical and
engineering processes. In incompressible flows, the periodic geometry allows to
compute the flow structure by solving the Navier-Stokes (NS) equations in the
minimal periodic cell of the structure, however large the pressure gradient.
Besides, when gas flow under large pressure drops are dealt with, the velocity
field is not periodic because of the density dependence on pressure. In this
case, the momentum balance equations must be solved numerically on the entire
channel, thereby requiring massive computational effort. Based on the marked
separation of scales between the length of the periodic cell and the overall
channel length characterizing many applications we develop a general method for
predicting both the large-scale pressure and velocity profiles, and the
small-scale flow structure. The approach proposed is based on the assumption
that the local dimensionless pressure drop as a function of the Reynolds
number, say $g({\rm Re})$, can be estimated from the solution of the
incompressible NS equations within the minimal periodic cell of the channel.
From the knowledge of $g({\rm Re})$, the pressure profile $P(Z)$ vs the large
scale axial coordinate $Z$ is derived analytically by quadratures. We show how
qualitatively different profiles $P(Z)$ can be obtained depending on the
equation of state the gas. The approach is validated by comparing the predicted
profiles with the full-scale numerical solution of the compressible NS
equations in different axially-symmetric periodic channel geometries.

</details>
